Songjiang County Committee Inspects the Seawall 116

The seawall of Punan County experienced a dangerous situation in autumn. After patrolman Li Yihua supervised the emergency repairs and reported to the county government, County Magistrate Jin accompanied a provincial committee to conduct an on-site inspection. After returning to the county seat, he convened leaders of various agencies to discuss repair methods and prepared an estimated budget, which has been submitted to the province for funding. Recently, the tide has risen again. County Magistrate Jin specially dispatched technician Zhao Shuda to inspect yesterday. Once the report is received, he will submit it to the province to urge for funding and start the repairs.

Male Corpse Discovered Outside Kunshan's Xiaoximen 117

An unidentified male corpse was discovered in the river near the Red Temple outside Xiaoximen in this city yesterday morning. There were many knife wounds. The village chief of the township, Shao Ruinian, reported to the First District Office, which forwarded the report to the county government for personnel to investigate. After receiving the report, County Magistrate Cheng immediately dispatched Judge Zhang Yizhi to bring back coroner Bu to conduct an examination. The deceased was found to be about 40 years old, with eight knife wounds on his head, a cross-shaped knife wound on the back of his head, and both arms and back were purplish-red. It was determined that he had been stabbed to death and thrown into the river before he died. The corpse tag was filled out, and no family members were found. The local guarantor, Li Zhiyi, was instructed to collect the body.

Suzhou's Wang Songliang Commits Suicide Over Marriage 118

Wang Songliang, a 22-year-old employee of the gift department of the Shanghai Mei Ya Silk Factory, was from Fenglin, Wuxing. His brother, Zhongfu, also works in the dyeing department of the factory as an accountant. Wang Songliang had a dispute with his mother over a marriage issue. He left for Suzhou without saying goodbye on the 29th of last month. He initially stayed at the Xin Su Tai Hotel outside Guanmen. When he left, he left a note at home saying that if the marriage did not succeed, he vowed not to return home. After Songliang arrived in Suzhou, he wrote a letter to his mother, still asking for permission for the marriage. He then received a reply from his mother, saying that everything could be discussed, there was no need to do this, he could have his freedom, and that his brother was sick in Shanghai and he should come to Shanghai quickly to visit and return home together. Unexpectedly, on the 30th, Songliang went to the China Hotel, opened Room 13, using the alias Chen Shuying. At 12:00 PM on the night of the first, the tea server Luo Liangquan discovered that Songliang was behaving strangely, as if he was about to commit suicide. He reported to the police precinct, which sent a police officer to transfer him to the hospital for treatment. It was found that he had not yet taken poison. The family members were notified immediately to come to Suzhou to claim him.

Disputes Over the Organization of a Labor Union at a Cotton Mill 119

Outside Panmen Gate, the Sulun Cotton Mill employs over 4,000 workers, making it the largest factory in Suzhou. About half a month ago, workers such as Guo A'ren and 50 others jointly submitted a petition to the County Party Headquarters, requesting permission to establish the Wu County Cotton Weaving Labor Union. The County Party Headquarters immediately issued an order to investigate the matter before further processing. However, two weeks passed without any investigators being dispatched. The factory learned of this and dismissed Guo A'ren. On the 30th, over 20 workers, including Tang A'yao, went to the County Party Headquarters to state that the workers had no motive to organize a labor union and that there were other forces at play. On the afternoon of the 1st, over 30 workers went to the County Party Headquarters, requesting a prompt approval of the labor union to avoid exploitation by the capitalists. They claimed that Tang A'yao and others were instigated by the capitalists. The official Gao Ziyan received them and promised to convey their intentions to the committee members. The workers then dispersed. The committee members of the Party Headquarters had divergent opinions on the matter, leading to heated debates during meetings without any resolution. Fearing that reactionary elements might cause trouble, the Public Security Bureau dispatched a large number of secret agents to conduct discreet investigations near the factory.

Three Fire Alarms in Wuxi in a Single Day 120

As winter arrives and the weather becomes dry, fire alarms are frequently heard. Yesterday alone, two fires occurred. Investigations revealed the following: (1) At Xu Shuntai Carpentry Workshop, located north of Yongding Bridge at the foot of the West Gate city wall, Xu A'gen runs a prosperous business. Yesterday, around 7 PM, an apprentice was cooking dinner under the stove, accidentally setting fire to the accumulated firewood, causing an uncontrollable blaze. Soon, the flames lit up the sky and spread rapidly. The Ruduan Fire Brigade arrived and extinguished the fire. However, six single-story buildings were completely destroyed, resulting in losses of several thousand yuan. (2) Outside the North Gate, in the open space near the railway bridge behind the Xinshichang market, north of Yunong Bridge, there were 40-odd thatched huts. Last night, around 9 PM, a fire unexpectedly broke out in the home of Wang Xiaosanqian, spreading to neighboring huts and piercing through the roofs. Various fire brigades were alerted and rushed to the scene, putting out the fire. However, many thatched huts were reduced to ashes. (3) At Sun Yuanmao Rattan Shop, located in Xiaozhu Lane under the bridge outside the North Gate, a fire suddenly broke out around 1 PM. Flames roared and thick smoke filled the air. Qian Shixiong, the police chief of the 5th branch of the Public Security Bureau, noticed the fire while on patrol. He called for help from Zhu Dehuai and Liu Yongsheng, two officers on duty with him. They broke into the shop and tried their best to extinguish the fire, preventing a major disaster. Only a portion of the rattan was burned. During the fire at the thatched huts near the railway, the 2nd section fire brigade of Guangqin District and the 7th section fire brigade of Sibao Bridge clashed while fighting the fire. As a result, firemen Shen A'er and Da Juzi from the Guangqin District sustained serious injuries. Zhou Wuda and Chen Yuanfa from the North 7th section were also seriously injured. The Joint Fire Fighting Association convened a meeting between the two sides to mediate and urged them not to create further conflict. Furthermore, a member of the Zhongdong Fire Brigade, for unknown reasons, got into a fight with Wang Huchen, a police officer petitioning at the Zhongdong Theater. The officer was severely injured and sent to the Brothers Hospital for treatment; his life may be in danger. Also, when the thatched huts caught fire, the flames reached the iron and power lines, causing considerable damage, resulting in a disruption of long-distance telephone communication between Nanjing and Shanghai, which is currently being repaired.

Opening of the Social Education Achievement Exhibition 121

The County Social Education Administrative Achievement Exhibition and the County Public School Achievement Exhibition, organized by the Wuxi County Education Bureau, opened yesterday at 1 PM at the County Library in the city center. A total of 24 social education institutions and 54 public schools participated, showcasing their achievements. The event was overseen and hosted by the general managers Hua Jingu, Chen Xianke, and Xu Zumo. Educational films will be shown today to add to the festivities.

Changshu Police Officer Commits Suicide by Shooting 122

Gao Wenchang, a third-class police officer stationed in Mocheng, Changshu, was from Shandong Province and was 35 years old. His younger brother, Gao Wenqing, served as a squad leader on a patrol ship in Changshu Town. Seven months ago, he was introduced by his elder brother to the police force as a probationary officer, and was officially made a third-class police officer just one week ago. Wenchang previously served in the military. Now stationed in Mocheng, he was often depressed due to financial difficulties. At noon on the first of this month, Gao Wenchang was on guard duty when he took the 7.9mm rifle he was holding, loaded a bullet, and committed suicide by pulling the trigger with his foot. The bullet entered his mouth and exited through his head, causing his teeth to fall out and his skull to explode, a truly horrific sight. The squad leader investigated the situation and determined that it was due to financial distress. He immediately reported it to the team headquarters and Gao Wenqing, his younger brother, and reported the case to the county government, who sent personnel to the countryside to investigate.

Robbery and Assault by Bandits in Sijing Township 123

In Hengjing Sijing Township, the third district, there is a widow named Shen Laotai, who is over fifty years old and has neither children nor many relatives. She recently sold unpolished rice and obtained 132 yuan. She lent out 100 yuan at interest, which was discovered by bandits. On the night of the 30th, more than ten bandits broke into Shen's home and searched for valuables, finding only 32 yuan and 200 copper coins. They then demanded to know where the remaining 100 yuan was hidden. Shen said she had lent it to someone else, but the bandits did not believe her. They used scissors to stab the old woman's left wrist, causing her to fall to the ground unconscious. The bandits then fled. The next morning, the local police team was informed. After investigating the situation, it appeared to be the work of local people. Suspects Jin Yinsheng and Shen Yishun were arrested and taken to the county for questioning on the 2nd.

Three Bandits Apprehended in the 19th District of Changzhou 124

Xie Yingzheng, the district chief of the 19th district of Wu County, upon noticing a series of robberies occurring within his jurisdiction, immediately directed the police and militia to conduct a thorough investigation. On the 28th of last month, they spotted Jiang Songgao, a resident of Tangshang, whose clothes were stained with blood and whose behavior was suspicious. They apprehended him, brought him in, and interrogated him. He confessed to participating in the robberies. On the 29th, they also apprehended robbers Zhu Fugeng and Lin Yuetang. District Chief Xie, together with the chief of the Xiaohe Public Security Branch, interrogated them strictly. The robbers confessed to robbing the homes of Shen Jinkou in Luoxiangli, Chen Hongfan in Jifu Township, and Sun Zhailong, and to spending the stolen goods. District Chief Xie and others continued to search for the remaining members of the gang. Yesterday (the 1st), they came to the county government to report the case and handed over the captured criminals to the county for questioning.

Dong Huaichuan of Nantong Arrested and Sent to the Province 125

Dong Huaichuan, the former leader of a detachment in the Jiangsu Provincial Maritime Patrol Team, resided in Nantong City after the team was disbanded. He was arrested by the Provincial Public Security Marine Police in Nantong for involvement in a kidnapping case in Shanghai, where he was identified as the ringleader by Shanghai detectives. He was escorted to the provincial capital and handed over to the Security Office for questioning. His accomplice, Fan Huagen, was also arrested by the county government on the 1st.

The Provincial Relief Committee Allocates Funds for Work Relief 126

The Jiangsu Provincial Relief Committee has allocated 40,000 yuan in relief funds to seven counties, including Nantong, with Nantong receiving 2,000 yuan, Taicang 2,000 yuan, Baoshan 6,000 yuan, Chuansha 8,000 yuan, Nanhui 6,000 yuan, Qidong 4,000 yuan, and Chongming 10,000 yuan, designated for work relief projects. On the 1st, the funds were handed over to the county magistrates for distribution.

Zhenjiang: Jiangsu Province to Establish Warehouses in Various Counties 127

Chen Guofu, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, recognizing the decline of rural areas and the economic exhaustion of various counties in recent years, is initiating the establishment of agricultural warehouses to alleviate rural financial problems. In addition to the resolution of the previous Rural Financial Relief Committee meeting, orders have been given to various counties to establish agricultural warehouses, and the Provincial Farmers' Bank has been instructed to raise funds. It is planned to establish 51 warehouses in various counties of the province, requiring a total of 1.2 million yuan. The Farmers' Bank has raised 600,000 yuan, but there is still a significant shortfall. Yang Fengshu, the acting head of the Farmers' Bank, was ordered to expedite the realization of this plan and recently went to various ports in Jiangsu and Shanghai to seek loans from the banking sector. It is reported that Director Yang returned to Zhenjiang last night to report on his mission. Various banks have agreed to provide short-term loans of 400,000 yuan, and instructions have been issued to various counties to actively prepare for the establishment of the warehouses.

Various Steamship Companies Add New Services 128

Competition in the Zhenjiang shipping industry is intensifying. Various steamship companies are adding new services. The Taichang Company is replacing the "Zhen Ning" ship with the "Xin Xing Tai" ship on the Ningkou route for long-term operation. It also plans to operate a newly renovated diesel ship, yet unnamed, between Fanchuan and Shaobo. The China Steamship Company plans to deploy the self-built "Jingde" ship, which is three stories high, 13 zhang long, with an iron hull and coal-fired engine. It has 16 rooms and can carry 1,000 passengers. It is stable and fast. It is said that the company will use it on the Ningkou route, with the expected launch date being at the end of the year.

Sixiang Qingtai Steamboat Caught Smuggling Opium 129

The Qingtai small steamboat operating between Beijing and Liuhe has been doing well since its launch. However, yesterday around 1 PM, as passengers disembarked after arriving in Liuhe from Beijing, a detective named Li noticed a crew member carrying a rattan basket, following the passengers ashore. Li approached and inspected the basket, finding it contained opium. He then dispatched officers to search the ship, discovering two more packages of opium and opium-smoking paraphernalia. The ship's accountant, Luo, and the crew members were taken into custody. Judge Yang held a court hearing and sentenced them to pay a fine and be released on bail.

Jiashan Madman Kills Mother and Sister 130

On the night of the 30th, a shocking incident occurred in Xigangtou, Xiadianmiao, in this county, where a madman brutally killed his mother and sister, drawing widespread attention. The details are as follows: In Xigangtou, there is a madman named Wang Aqi. His father, Dada, died early. His mother, Jiang, is 69 years old. Jiang had six children. The eldest daughter, Lanbao (one of the deceased), was 38 years old and married Yu Amao of Xicun. After her husband's death, she lived with her mother and helped with household chores. The second daughter is married to Xu Awu. The third son, Jinsheng, is 29 years old and married. The fourth son is Aqi, 25 years old, who is married to a woman surnamed Tang but has no children. The fifth son, Adi, and the sixth son, Qiuquan, are both young. They are farmers and make kiln blanks as a side business. The family is very poor. However, starting from his grandfather, the family has had a history of mental illness, although not very severe. This condition was inherited through three generations, becoming worse in Aqi's case. Aqi was quite sincere and diligent after his marriage four years ago. Unexpectedly, he suddenly developed madness the following year. Initially, it was mild, occurring intermittently. At the same time, his third elder brother, Jinsheng, and his eldest sister, Lanbao, also suffered from the same illness. As a result, three madmen lived under one roof, causing unrest. The two younger brothers and the daughter-in-law, Tang, moved to relatives' homes, leaving only the old mother and sister Lanbao to manage the household. In recent days, Aqi's madness has worsened. He claimed to be possessed by a high-ranking official, talking nonsense incessantly. Sometimes, he would wield a kitchen knife randomly, causing everyone to run away. Before long, Lanbao became bedridden due to illness, and the old mother was tending to her by her side. Who knew that a tragic incident would occur at this time? On the night of the 30th, Aqi suddenly grabbed a stone hammer and rushed to Lanbao's bedside, killing Lanbao. He then grabbed his old mother, stuffed her mouth with bamboo chopsticks and a scrubbing brush to prevent her from making noise, and then repeatedly struck her with the hammer. He dragged her to the riverbank and pushed her into the river. At that time, dawn was approaching. Knowing he had committed a crime, the madman fled far away. On the morning of the 1st, men and women from far and near gathered, and they found the body of a woman lying on the ground, with many severe injuries to her head, waist, and chest, and blood everywhere. At the same time, they found a floating female body at the mouth of Shatuo Port, which was the madman's mother, Jiang. The scene was extremely cruel. After committing the crime, the madman fled to the home of his sister's husband, Xu Awu, in Poxuegang. He was apprehended by the captain of the local security team, Lv Huanchen, and imprisoned in heavy shackles. He was still babbling and constantly mentioning the high-ranking official. Captain Lv reported the case to the court, while the local community reported it to the court, requesting an autopsy.

Robbery at Baihe Nunnery in Ningbo 131

The Baihe Nunnery in Gaoxiantian, Yindong, is an ancient temple from the Ming Dynasty. The abbess, Yi Ying, is in her forties and has considerable savings. Unexpectedly, around 3 AM last night, six bandits broke in, ransacking the place. It is estimated that they stole cash and miscellaneous items worth 200-300 gold pieces. The abbess has reported the incident to the police in Wuxiang, requesting their investigation.

Mass Rally Held Yesterday in This City to Condemn the Rebels; Over 100,000 Attendees from All Sectors of the Party, Government, and Military; Telegrams Sent Nationwide Unanimously Denouncing the Illegal Organization; Central Committee Members from Various Regions Invited to Come to Beijing to Discuss National Affairs 132

Chairman's Report 136

After opening the meeting and observing customary rituals, Chairman Lu Jingshi reported that the Shanghai citizens' rally to condemn the rebels was being held today, with enthusiastic participation from citizens from all sectors of agriculture, industry, commerce, and education, demonstrating a shared spirit of indignation and hatred. He noted that today, the nation is facing a grave crisis with internal and external pressures. The international situation is becoming increasingly tense. China should strive to develop its national strength, eliminate bandits, and engage in production in order to avoid the disaster of national subjugation. Although differing political views are common, in the face of great difficulties, we must set aside minor grievances and jointly undertake major tasks. However, Chen Mingshu and others have brazenly betrayed the nation and the people, mixing in with all reactionary elements such as the Third Party, the Social Democratic Party, the BA Group, and the Nationalist faction, establishing a false government, turning from resisting Japan to being pro-Japan, and from suppressing the communists to collaborating with them, acting as tools for red and white imperialists to damage the national foundation. The so-called People's Government is just as comical as the puppet regime in Manchukuo. Since the incident, the Communist Party, which is deeply hated by the Chinese people, has openly filled Fujian Province, engaged in red terror, deprived the people of all freedoms, and created war. As a result, the people's suffering has deepened and the nation's international standing has declined. Their betrayal of the country and harm to the people is greater than anyone else. The 19th Route Army has destroyed its former glorious history and its oath not to participate in the civil war, which we deeply regret. Now that Chen's rebellion is evident, the people of the whole country must unanimously condemn it and quickly quell the rebellion in order to save the Party and the nation.

Summary of Speeches 137

Next, Tao Baichuan delivered a speech, stating that today's Shanghai citizens' rally to condemn the rebels has two goals: First, to deny the legitimacy of the People's Government; and second, to overthrow the rebellious party and the traitors. The People's Government, as its name suggests, should be organized by the people, but it is only supported by a small number of people. What we need now is (1) Peace, so that all sectors of agriculture, industry, commerce, and education can live and work in peace; (2) Unity, so that the nation can become strong under a unified government; (3) Construction, to achieve national revival; (4) Suppression of bandits, as the false government in Fujian is actively colluding with communist bandits; and (5) Resistance to Japan, to seek national survival. If these five goals are not vigorously pursued, the rebels will undoubtedly engage in sabotage. Therefore, we must eliminate the People's Government and destroy the 19th Route Army. Lu Wenshao then gave a speech, stating that the 19th Route Army, which was once admired by all sectors as a national hero, is now forcibly organizing a People's Government in Fujian, causing military disaster and undermining unity. The citizens of Shanghai should vigorously support the central government and eliminate the rebels in order to seek happiness for the people. Next, the Fujian Provincial Alliance to Protect the Party and Condemn the Rebels (Gan Yun) spoke, stating that the People's Government of Fujian destroyed the Party's national flag and the leader's portrait, which is extremely heartbreaking. We must only fight against the rebels in order to protect this revolutionary history.

Resolutions Passed 138

Meeting Declaration 139

To be forwarded by various newspapers to all compatriots across the country for your public knowledge. When red bandits ran rampant and strong neighbors invaded, the nation and the people were in a perilous state. The central government, after much deliberation, deeply understood that it was necessary to first secure the interior before resisting foreign aggression and that there was no way to save the nation without suppressing the bandits. Therefore, the military was reorganized and a large-scale campaign was launched. Now that the long-standing threat of the bandits entering Jiangxi had been cleared and the sweeping operation was expected to be completed, it was thought that the nation's future would be revealed. Unexpectedly, Chen Mingshu, Li Jishen, Chen Youren, and others, being mad and depraved, took advantage of the nation's internal and external troubles, colluding with corrupt elements such as the Social Democratic Party, the Third Party, the Nationalist faction, the Communist Party, and old warlords to organize the so-called Production Party and People's Revolutionary Government in Fuzhou, abolishing the national title, changing the national emblem without authorization, and openly betraying the Party and the nation. Instead, they have become insane and are acting against the tide, doing things that are neither donkey nor horse. The content is even more complex and bizarre. Sun Ke Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning - Says Political Solution to Fujian Incident is Hopeless - Central Government's Choice of Personnel to Go South is Undecided - Implementing Open Governance is Not Far Off 142

Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, arrived in Shanghai by night train from Nanjing at 7:30 yesterday morning. The content of his conversation is recorded as follows:

Political Solution Is Out of the Question 143

Sun said that the central government originally intended to resolve the Fujian Incident through political means and was unwilling to resort to military force lightly. However, based on the current situation, a political solution is out of the question. The military aspect also depends on the situation. The central government troops in Zhejiang are temporarily adopting a defensive posture. If Fujian attacks Zhejiang, then war is inevitable. Otherwise, if Fujian does not invade Zhejiang, then a temporary truce is possible. However, it is uncertain whether there will be other solutions in the future.

No News of Hu's Forming a Government 144

When reporters asked about the attitude of Guangdong and Guangxi and the rumor that Hu Hanmin was forming a new government, Sun said that the attitude of Guangdong and Guangxi was as reported in the newspapers. As for Hu Hanmin forming a third government, he had not heard of it. But the country has reached this point, and further division is unacceptable.

Open Governance is Not Far Off 145

It was reported that Central Committee members staying in Shanghai, such as Mr. Li Liejun, had contributed a proposal for reforming the central government's politics to the authorities, but Nanjing had not seen any suggestions from Li and others, so it was not discussed. Three Unified Taxes Increased - To Be Implemented from the 5th 162

Ta Kung Pao says: The Ministry of Finance believes that the national treasury is currently in deficit, and major construction projects and the suppression of bandits all require large amounts of funds. In order to make overall plans, it is proposed to increase the unified taxes on cement, matches, and cigarettes appropriately. The proposal has been submitted to the Executive Yuan for a meeting and approved. It is scheduled to be implemented uniformly from the 5th of this month. The Taxation Department has already notified various merchants. The revised new tax rules obtained by the Ta Kung Pao reporter are as follows:

Cigarettes 163

For domestically produced paper cigarettes, those with a selling price of more than 300 yuan per 50,000 cigarettes will be in the first class and will be taxed at 160 yuan. Those with a selling price of less than 300 yuan per 50,000 cigarettes will be in the second class and will be taxed at 80 yuan. The highest selling price for the second class may be relaxed by 20 yuan if it is not the location of the cigarette factory, that is, the highest selling price per box in other cities must not exceed 320 yuan. There is no limit to the highest selling price for the first class. This new tax rate will be implemented on December 5th of this year. From that date, domestically produced paper cigarettes will not be allowed to leave the factory without new tax stamps. Cigarettes that have left the factory with old tax stamps before November 5th will still be allowed to be sold uniformly. The old tax stamps purchased and stored by various cigarette companies should be exchanged for new stamps at the price within 30 days of the implementation of the tax increase.

Matches 164

(1) Sulfurized phosphorus matches: Class A box size: length 48, width 33, thickness 14 mm, each small box containing 75 to 80 matches or less will be taxed at 10 yuan and 8 jiao. Class B box size: length 48, width 34, thickness 16 mm, each small box containing 100 to 105 matches or less will be taxed at 13 yuan and 5 jiao. (2) Safety matches: Class A box size: length 48, width 34, thickness 16 mm, each small box containing 75 to 80 matches or less will be taxed at 13 yuan and 5 jiao. Class B box size: length 59, width 38, thickness 18 mm, each small box containing 100 to 105 matches or less will be taxed at 17 yuan and 4 jiao. Class C box size: length 59, width 40, thickness 18 mm, each small box containing 115 to 120 matches or less will be taxed at 21 yuan.

Cement 165

The unified cement tax, originally set at 6 jiao per barrel weighing 170 kilograms, is now revised to 1 yuan and 2 jiao in national currency. Those packaged in bags should be calculated at double the original tax according to their weight.

Cigarette Industry Petitions for Postponement of Tax Increase 166

The local cigarette factories believe that private cigarettes are spreading widely in various provinces, and the government has not yet taken measures to rectify the situation, but has issued an order to increase taxes, which will be implemented on the 5th of this month. Those with a selling price of more than 300 yuan per 50,000 cigarettes will be in the first class and will be taxed at 160 yuan. Those with a selling price of more than 300 yuan per 50,000 cigarettes will be in the Class Cigarettes and will be taxed at 80 yuan. Each cigarette factory believes that as the tax rate increases, private cigarettes will also become more prevalent, and cigarette merchants' businesses will feel even more distressed. Therefore, the Shanghai Chinese Cigarette Factory Industry Association held a meeting for discussion. It was decided that the government should be asked to review the current state of the cigarette industry, first clear out private cigarettes to avoid infringing on legitimate businesses, and the new cigarette tax rate should be postponed. When private cigarettes are eliminated in the future, the tax increase will be discussed again. Lao Jingxiu, Ding Boquan, Shen Xingde, Bao Yingsheng, and Wu Linzhi were elected as petition representatives. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the representatives first went to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to request support for the petition to the financial authorities to postpone the implementation of the new tax. Tong Fuhui, the representative of the foreign cigarette factory, also went to the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance to petition. The petition is recorded as follows: I am writing to inform you that we received a public letter from the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance on the 1st of this month, stating that the Ministry of Finance has ordered that the national treasury is currently in deficit, and major construction projects and the suppression of bandits all require large amounts of funds. The tax rate of the cigarette unified tax in our country is still low, and it should be appropriately increased. All paper cigarettes made by the state with a selling price of more than 300 yuan per 50,000 cigarettes will be in the first class and will be taxed at 160 yuan. All paper cigarettes made by the state with a selling price of less than 300 yuan per 50,000 cigarettes will be in the first class and will be taxed at 80 yuan. The right to increase taxes is indeed in the hands of the government, but the business of merchants should not be infringed upon, which is also the government's responsibility. At present, private cigarettes are rampant and spreading widely. In these three years, their monthly sales have increased from one or two boxes to more than ten thousand boxes, and there is a tendency to increase day by day. However, the government has not taken effective measures to suppress and rectify these tax-evading cigarettes, which has damaged the legitimate businesses of cigarette merchants and caused them to decline day by day. We seek relief, but instead, we are issued a tax increase order, which will cause cigarette merchants' businesses to stagnate invisibly. As the tax rate increases, private cigarettes will also become more prevalent, and the businesses of legitimate cigarette merchants will also decline further. Therefore, the government will start by increasing taxes and end up by reducing taxes, causing both the public and private sectors to suffer and not benefiting the real situation. Therefore, in order to make overall plans, we should first formulate regulations for rectifying private cigarettes and carry out rectification first. After private cigarettes are brought under control, we can discuss the tax increase again. Then the businesses of cigarette merchants will not be infringed upon, and even if the tax rate increases gradually, they will be able to bear it. Otherwise, if the businesses are dying, even the government's tax revenue will decrease as a result, which is not a good way for both parties. If the government needs funds urgently and must increase taxes, it also needs to examine the current state of the cigarette industry and increase the rate appropriately, so that the tax revenue will improve and there will be no damage to the business, so that the national economy and the people's livelihood will benefit from it. Our association, in response to the requests of various associations, has specially dispatched Lao Jingxiu, Ding Boquan, Shen Xingde, Bao Yingsheng, and Wu Linzhi as representatives to send a copy of the petition to the Ministry of Finance. We respectfully petition your department (association), hoping that the director (association) will show sympathy for the merchants' difficulties and promptly forward to the Ministry of Finance that all newly ordered cigarette tax rates should be implemented after redrawing and rectifying private cigarettes, so as to maintain the business of cigarette merchants. This is a public petition. Ministry of Finance Taxation Department, Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Shanghai Chinese Cigarette Factory Industry Association, December 2, 22.

(4) To publish a declaration. The "Fujian Overseas Chinese Rescue Association Declaration" was approved. "We, the people of Fujian, have suffered from natural and man-made disasters in recent years. Although we are living an inhuman life, we still want to be "human." Especially in the current serious situation, if we, the people of Fujian, want to survive and enjoy, we must first ask ourselves if we want to be human and whether we want to clean up the gathering place for being human. The will of the people is the power of society. The chaos in society depends entirely on whether the people have healthy power to eliminate it. The reason why Fujian has suffered so much in recent years is due to the corruption of warlords and communists. However, the lack of unity among the people of Fujian is also to blame. The people of Fujian in the past, although in deep water and scorching fire, could still find a way to survive. But now, the people of Fujian are about to face the crisis of the collapse of their hometown and the destruction of their families, and there is no way to survive. Should we just sit and wait for death? Especially we, the Fujian Overseas Chinese who are away from our hometown, feel even more desolate. The 19th Army, the hero of the Anti-Japanese War, is the army that we, the Fujian Overseas Chinese, love the most. We warmly welcome the 19th Army to build a new Fujian and to relieve the suffering of the people of Fujian. We did not expect that the 19th Army would give Fujian the policy of destroying Fujian and harming the people. We sincerely welcome the 19th Army to eliminate the communists in Fujian Province and to protect the livelihood of the people of Fujian. Reduced Postage for Parcels to Hong Kong and Macau 169

According to postal service news, the postage for parcels sent to Hong Kong and Macau has now been reduced as follows: Hong Kong (effective November 1 of this year): 63 cents in foreign currency per kilogram, 2.15 yuan in foreign currency for 5 kilograms, 2.30 yuan in foreign currency for 10 kilograms. Macau (effective January 1 of next year): 63 cents in foreign currency per kilogram, 1.15 yuan in foreign currency for 5 kilograms, 2.30 yuan in foreign currency for 10 kilograms, 3.45 yuan in foreign currency for 15 kilograms, 4.60 yuan in foreign currency for 20 kilograms. Parcels to Macau were originally limited to 10 kilograms in weight. Starting January 1 of next year, the limit will be increased to 20 kilograms.

In order to jointly address the decline of the silk industry, silk factories and trade associations in Jiangsu and Zhejiang held their second joint meeting in Shanghai yesterday to discuss solutions. Details are as follows:

Attending Representatives 171

Representatives from silk factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang who attended yesterday: Zhang Yunsheng, Shi Xinsheng, Sun Yingchang, Zhang Chucai, Chen Liezhong, Shen Huachen, Zhu Zhuxian, Zhang Peishen, and Mao Yiqun from the Shanghai Silk Factories Trade Association; Chu Liseng and Jiang Laixian from the Zhejiang Silk Factories Trade Association; Qian Fenghao, Cheng Bingruo, and Ye Cangfu from the Wuxi Silk Factories Trade Association. Silk merchants have reached the point of bankruptcy. The trade associations in Shanghai, Wuxi, and Zhejiang, seeking to remedy the situation, are holding joint meetings to discuss fundamental solutions. Today is the second meeting. The draft articles of association for the silk exchange have been prepared and are being submitted for review, as well as for the joint expression of opinions and discussion of concrete methods.

Resolutions of Various Proposals 173

After Jin Xi Was Arrested, His Family Submitted Nationality Certificates; Three Lawyers Were Hired to Handle Legal Procedures 174

On October 5 of the eighteenth year of the Republic, Jin Xi, along with his father Jin Yongduo (also known as Jin Che), naturalized as Chinese citizens and obtained Chinese nationality. On the afternoon of the twelfth day of last month, at around 6:00 PM, he left home, saying he was going to meet a friend, but did not return that night. The next day, his family learned that he had been arrested by police dispatched by the Japanese Consulate in Shanghai in the French Concession. Citizens of this city, including Li Songnian, Yang Shichang, and Zhang Yiqing, argued that since Jin Xi had acquired Chinese nationality, the French Concession police authorities should provide him with legal protection. They also sent letters to legal entities such as the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the French Concession Chinese Ratepayers' Association to jointly protest and demand that the municipal government conduct a stern negotiation. The municipal government stated that it needed to first verify whether Jin Xi had indeed acquired Chinese nationality before it could proceed. Now, Jin Xi's family has hired three lawyers, Huai Yunmei, Gong Jie, and Luo Zhaoxin, to handle the legal procedures, and has submitted a copy of Jin Xi's naturalization certificate. From this, it can be known that Jin Xi is indeed of Chinese nationality and should receive the protection of Chinese law. His arrest without cause not only harms his personal legal rights, but also infringes on the sovereignty of our country. It is heard that legal entities in this city will exert their utmost efforts to protest.

Shanghai Maritime Customs Notice on Scheduled Implementation of the New System of Weights and Measures; To Be Implemented from January 1, 1934 175

Shanghai Maritime Customs issued Notice No. 1328 yesterday regarding the implementation of the new system of weights and measures, as ordered. The notice stated: "As per the Ministry of Finance's order that all maritime customs across the country shall implement the new system of weights and measures starting February 1, 1934, we must comply accordingly. All merchants involved are to immediately notify foreign manufacturers and shipping merchants with whom they have relations that all markings and invoices for goods destined for China must be converted to the new system of weights and measures to avoid inconvenience upon arrival of the goods at the port. If any merchants have any uncertainties regarding this matter, they may apply to the Customs Valuation Department for clarification. All are to be fully informed. This notice."

Major Lee Fray of the American Relief Effort, Who Exerted the Most Effort to Aid Chinese Disasters, Has Passed Away; A Great Loss for Chinese Disaster Victims 178

According to the Shanghai Evening Post & Mercury, the American Advisory Committee for Disaster Relief in this city received a telegram from New York today (the 2nd) stating that Major Lee Fray, who exerted the most effort in the United States to raise donations to aid Chinese disasters, suddenly passed away in New York on the 30th of last month. Since 1928, Lee has served as the National Director of the American Committee for Relief in China. The committee is located on East 41st Street in New York. Although it is headed by Bai Huairen, who previously visited China to inspect the disaster situation, all fundraising matters are planned and executed by Lee. Therefore, he was recognized as the brains and power of the committee. During this time of economic decline in the United States, without Lee's enthusiastic fundraising efforts, it would have been difficult to obtain so many donations that flowed into China. For example, in the most recent two months, the committee remitted money to the Yellow River Disaster Relief Association four times, each time with US$5,000, which was also the result of Lee's leadership. His death is not only a loss to the world and philanthropists, but also a loss of a good friend to countless disaster victims in China.

Brokerage Business License Fee Changed to 200 National Currency Yuan 179

The Social Affairs Bureau conveyed an order to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, stating that it had received Instruction No. 20811 from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. The instruction stated that the business license fee for stock exchange brokers, previously set at 100 yuan in national currency by a ministerial order in July of the 15th year of the Republic according to Article 20 of the Implementing Regulations of the Stock Exchange Law, has been in effect for over three years. Given the current situation, it is necessary to adjust the original fee amount. Therefore, the business license fee for brokers is hereby changed to 200 yuan in national currency. All provincial and municipal governments are to be notified for their information, and all relevant departments are to be notified to disseminate the information. This order is for the bureau to notify the chamber of commerce for compliance. This order.

Recent News from the Hongkou People's Obstetrics Hospital 180

The founders of the Hongkou People's Obstetrics Hospital, including Du Yuesheng, Gu Shaoqing, Zhang Xiaolin, Wang Boyuan, and Weng Guoxun, are sparing no effort to protect the health of the common people. Recently, due to the domestic commercial recession, male and female laborers are feeling the impact. If they become ill, they will inevitably be unable to afford medical treatment. Therefore, in addition to providing normal medical and pharmaceutical services at the old hospital site on Tongzhou Road, patients sent by various factories or group organizations for diagnosis and treatment are treated free of charge. If the illness is severe and hospitalization and medication are required, no fees are charged. Therefore, the number of people seeking treatment is extremely high, averaging 70-80 people per day. The new hospital behind the Tilanqiao police station also provides diagnosis and medication. Childbirth is free for poor pregnant women. If fees are charged, they are extremely economical, in order to save money and provide relief.

Liu and Yang's Marriage Gone Wrong; Groom (Whose Name Meant Monk) Missed the Wedding Date; Bride Became a Nun and Refused to Marry 181

Yang Qingxiang from Tongdong works as a salesman at a flower shop in Nanshi. He has two daughters. His second daughter, Yinbao, is currently 22 years old. When she was 18, her father arranged a marriage through a matchmaker to He Shang (meaning Monk), the son of Liu Zhaokui from Chuansha, who runs a coffin shop business on Nancang Street. It was once planned to marry her off during an auspicious date in August of the 20th year of the Republic, but in the spring of that year, He Shang had a disagreement with his father and then ran away, and his whereabouts were unknown. Liu searched everywhere, but there was no news. When the scheduled wedding date arrived, Liu saw that He Shang had not returned home and immediately informed the matchmaker to notify the bride's family to postpone the wedding. When Yang found out that the wedding was a major event, that the selected auspicious day could not be changed, and that all the dowry and other preparations were already complete, he questioned Liu about the reason. Liu had no choice but to tell him that He Shang had run away and that people were being sent to look for him. They would select another auspicious date to hold the wedding after he returned home. Nearly two years have passed, and He Shang still has not returned. At the beginning of last month, He Shang suddenly returned home. Liu was overjoyed and immediately informed the bride's family, and selected New Year's Day next year as the auspicious date for the wedding. When Yang found out, he told his daughter about the wedding date. But Yinbao thought that He Shang was too absurd about the major event of marriage, and wondered how she would live if he ran away again after they were married. Therefore, she expressed her unwillingness to marry He Shang. She has now decided to become a nun in a nunnery to practice her religion. The day before yesterday, after writing a letter, she ran away. That evening, her mother did not see Yinbao return home and became very worried. Suddenly, she found the letter in a drawer and gave it to Yang to read. They were shocked and immediately sent people to search for her in the nunneries in the north and south, and also sent the girl's letter to the Liu family. When Liu saw the letter, he gave it to He Shang to read and scolded him severely. He Shang was very remorseful and did not know how to resolve the situation.

Japanese Women Organized Smuggling Ring; Japanese Women Used Thighs to Secretly Transport Metals and Contraband 184

According to yesterday's Japanese-language Mainichi Shimbun, an international smuggling ring organized by top jewel and precious metal merchants in Shanghai, Dalian, Kobe, Osaka, Yokohama, and Tokyo, in connection with a Frenchman named Takra, has been investigated by the Tokyo Metropolitan Police Department, and the criminals have been arrested one after another. Man's Corpse Found with Eight Knife Wounds; Abandoned Land on Lincoln Road in Western Shanghai; Suicide Note Unrelated, Suspected of Being a Moved Corpse 186

At approximately 6:10 AM yesterday morning, an assassinated male corpse was suddenly discovered in the abandoned land on Lincoln Road in Western Shanghai's Zhoujiaqiao. There were as many as seven or eight knife wounds to the neck and shoulders. The scene was bloody and gruesome. The details are recorded below:

Assassinated Male Corpse Discovered 187

At approximately 6:00 AM yesterday, an assassinated male corpse was discovered on the abandoned land on Lincoln Road in Western Shanghai, approximately one li west of Shenxin School. After a villager saw it while passing by, he immediately reported it to Wang Zhixiang, a volunteer police officer at the Huafeng Type Foundry, who in turn reported it to the Zhoujiaqiao Sixth District Precinct.

Investigation of Injury Situation 188

Upon receiving the report, Precinct Officer Wei Jiechen immediately went to investigate. It was found that the assassinated, unnamed male corpse was approximately 23-24 years old, wearing a blue wool camel hair robe, gray wool serge pants, light gray gauze socks with no shoes, a shaved head, a slightly long face, and gold teeth in his mouth. He resembled a gangster. There was a three-inch-long knife wound on the right side of his neck. There were six or seven knife wounds on the back of his head and shoulders. The scene was bloody and gruesome. A murder weapon and a torn letter were found on the ground near the corpse. Two pawn tickets and eight small foreign coins were found in his pocket. After the investigation, he immediately reported the details to District Chief Tan of the Sixth District and ordered Xin Fu, the land guard of the area, to report to the local court for an inquest.

Unrelated Letter Found 189

Sixth District Internal Affairs Officer Yin Dengdi found that the letter was addressed to student Ding Tingsheng at Shenxin School, and its contents were words of gifting food. He immediately sent police to the Shenxin workshop and summoned Ding Tingsheng and his father Ding Huaiqing for questioning. According to Ding Huaiqing, 49 years old and from Wuxi, Tingsheng is my son. The letter was written by a friend who was sending something. Tingsheng put it in his pocket. Last night, Tingsheng and a certain gentleman were walking on Lincoln Road when he used the letter to wipe his nose and threw it on the road. He did not know the deceased, etc. Ding Tingsheng's statement was the same. After hearing their statements, District Officer Xing determined that they were not related and ordered their release pending further investigation.

Inquest Indicates Corpse Was Moved 190

The local court then dispatched Prosecutor Li to the scene for an inquest. The inquest found that the unnamed murdered male corpse had indeed been killed by knife wounds during his lifetime. It appeared that he was murdered and then his body was moved and abandoned here. A photograph was taken and the local land guard was ordered to prepare a coffin for burial, and to await the strict arrest and investigation of the murderers.

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, the Ministry of Finance plans to increase the unified tax on matches, cigarettes, and cement. However, the British-American Tobacco Company has not yet made a decision due to the strike. Chinese tobacco factories will also express their sympathy. The details of each item are recorded as follows:

Purchase and Manufacture of Vehicles 195

Since extending its routes this summer, the Chinese Merchants' Electric Tram Company has found that its original vehicles are insufficient for distribution. The No. 4 tram line between Nanyang Bridge and Gaochang Temple, and the No. 2 tram line on the Inner and Outer Circular Roads, pass between Shangwen Gate and Daxing Street, which only has single tracks, causing the trams to wait for a long time. Costing 500,000 197

As for the reconstruction of double tracks at Gaochang Temple, it will be carried out only after the completion of the projects on the other lines. Road construction at Lujiabang is difficult to achieve in the short term because the Public Works Bureau's road filling project has not yet been properly completed. It is now scheduled to convene female university students who are interested in the Young Women's Christian Association on the 8th, 9th, and 13th of this month for a symposium. Ms. Ding Shujing, the general secretary of the association, also took a car to Beiping yesterday to attend the meeting. It is also reported that Ms. Ding will travel to various parts of North China to inspect the work progress of the city, school, and rural associations, and will return to Shanghai around the end of the month.

The Dispute Over the Auction of Huang Chu Jiu's Real Estate and Tongde Medical College; The Court Should Provide Fair Relief 202

Recently, the Shanghai Second Special District Local Court auctioned Huang Chu Jiu's real estate, including the self-built buildings of Tongde Medical College, which caused objections from Tongde Medical College. However, the school is a famous academic institution and charitable organization in this city. What are the details? The society pays close attention to it. The investigation is as follows: Tongde Medical College was originally located on Maigen Road. In the 15th year of the Republic of China, when Huang Chu Jiu was the chairman of the school board, he leased his private property at No. 10441 of the British Registered Deed on Tongfu Road, along with a Western-style house on the ground, to the college. He also allowed the college to build school buildings, wards, etc. on the open space there. The college spent its own money to build two six-story buildings and seventeen bungalows. It also renovated and decorated the original Western-style house to suit the needs of the hospital and college. It also installed water and electricity projects, and spent about 57,000 yuan on repairs over the years. At that time, Huang Chu Jiu had an oral agreement to donate the base and the original Western-style house to the school, but due to debt relations, he did not hand them over in time. Unfortunately, Huang Chu Jiu died of illness two years ago. His family continued Huang's old wishes and allowed all construction, improvement, and repair costs to be repaid first in the future. Later, due to the liquidation of the Gongfa Company, the base was also part of the Gongfa Company's liquidation and was auctioned by the court. In order to protect all property rights, Tongde Medical College submitted a statement to the Second Special District Local Court, requesting that priority repayment be reserved during the auction, and was approved to record the matter in the auction announcement. However, the auction announcement did not specify it separately, so Tongde Medical College specially published a notice to solemnly clarify to avoid misunderstanding. It is found that Tongde Medical College and its affiliated hospital have been seeking expansion since Gu Yuqi became the president, adding research rooms and adding various instruments to facilitate students' practice. Therefore, the number of male and female students has increased to more than 250. Shao Lizi has also been elected as the chairman of the school board, and Chu Minyi, Sun Zhesheng, Zhu Jiahua, Pan Gongzhan, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Zhang Xiaolin and other gentlemen are the school board members. All school board members are leaders who are making every effort to promote new medicine and charitable undertakings. The future of the college is limitless. The court must also provide fair legal relief. It is also heard that the college, based on the relationship of lease and surface rights, has the right to use the self-built houses, water and electricity projects, etc. for at least 20 years. This legal right should not only be bound by the current lessor, but also by the purchaser of the property.

Hu Die Requests to Revoke the Trademark Contract 207

Huanan Chemical Industry Company, located at No. 4 Renshou Lane, Annejin Road, French Concession, signed a contract with Ms. Hu Die, a famous movie star in Shanghai, on June 4 last year, using Hu Die's name and portrait as trademarks for five kinds of cosmetics, such as snow cream, face powder, tooth powder, toothpaste, and perfume, and submitted an application for registration to the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. When the contract was signed, the two parties agreed on the terms that 1% of the total surplus of goods sold each year would be given to Hu as remuneration, and a cash payment of 2,500 yuan would be made. It was also noted that if no products were sold on the market one year after the contract was signed, the contract should be invalidated. When the contract was signed, Huanan Company invited lawyer Zha Renwei, and Hu's side invited lawyer Feng Xizui to the scene to sign and prove it. After the contract was signed, Huanan Company produced a kind of tooth powder. On the front of the packaging bag, Hu Die's portrait was printed, and the words "Tooth Powder" were written below, but the name of the product and the trademark name were not noted. Advertisements were published in various newspapers, but it was written that Hu Die's name and portrait were used as trademarks. Later, Family Industrial Company learned that the Hu Die tooth powder produced by Huanan Company was confusing with the name of Family Industrial Company's Invincible Brand tooth powder with the butterfly as its trademark, and issued a statement in the newspaper and filed a complaint with the Trademark Bureau. The two parties were involved in litigation and opened a war of words. It was seen in various newspapers. Since then, Huanan Company has only produced tooth powder, and the remaining four kinds of goods with Hu Die as the trademark have not been released and sold on the market. Now, Hu Die's side believes that since Huanan Company has been signing the contract for more than a year, and no goods have been produced and sold, the contract should be terminated according to the agreed terms. Therefore, lawyer Feng Xizui sent a letter to Sun Zijiang, the manager of Huanan Company, requesting the revocation of the signed contract. However, Huanan Company has not made any concrete indication since receiving the letter. Hu Die had no choice but to entrust lawyer Feng to file a complaint with the Civil Court of the Second Special District Local Court to request the revocation of the contract with Huanan Company. After the court sent the summons according to the complaint, the defendant also invited lawyers Zhang Shizhao and Peng Yuanxun to file a defense. Yesterday, Judge Wu Xiaoke summoned both parties to the Civil Court No. 7 of the Second Special District Court. The lawyers representing both parties appeared in court. After the court briefly questioned the agents of both parties, it was announced that evidence still needed to be investigated, and the officer ordered to wait for a scheduled summons for further interrogation.

Forging Signatures to Buy Sand Field Case; Ling Yunsu Denies Collusion; Court Orders the Plaintiff to Appear in Person 212

Ling Yunzhai, an elderly man over seventy years old, is from Gaoqiao, Pudong. He recently hired lawyers Yin Shijie and Wang Weizhen to file a complaint with the Criminal Court of the Local Court against Kuang Zhongmou and Lu Yangchun, the owners of the Lai Market, for forging signatures, requesting legal action, and filing a collateral civil lawsuit. The statement briefly stated that the plaintiff purchased 26 mu, 3 fen, 6 li, and 5 hao of tidal land in Chunyi Gaoqiao Township from the Sand Field Bureau of the Ministry of Finance on August 17 of the 11th year of the Republic of China, and obtained the No. 9969 Su Sha Ling Ji Hu Cai Bureau license of the Ministry of Finance, and had legally paid grain and managed the property. Later, due to business, the document was mortgaged to the second defendant for several years. Repeatedly asked the agent to redeem it, but they all kept delaying. Unexpectedly, the Land Bureau recently cleared up the old case of rat sand (i.e., Gaoqiao sand). The first defendant actually erected stone boundaries on the land in the name of Yongning Company, claiming that it belonged to him. The plaintiff negotiated with the first defendant, who claimed that he had purchased it from the plaintiff and submitted a book printed by him (the property evidence submitted by Yongning Company), which actually contained a photo of the document and a photo of the official sale contract, each on one page. Looking closely at the sale contract (the date of the sale contract was April of the 13th year), under the name of Ling Runji, there was an unrecognizable flourish, with the small characters "Dai Ya" (代押) below. It was extremely shocking. The plaintiff had never issued this document, and he always used the seal with the two characters "Yunzhai" (雲齋) in seal script to show good faith. This signature was forged. It was obvious that the first and second defendants colluded to forge the signature, harming the plaintiff. If legal action is not taken, how can evil be deterred and property rights protected? Their actions constitute a crime under Article 234, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law and a collateral civil lawsuit to confirm that the purchase is invalid. The court had previously held a hearing that was not concluded. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Sun Jikang continued the trial. The plaintiff did not appear, and lawyer Yin Shijie appeared on his behalf. The defendant Kuang Zhongmou and his lawyer also appeared in court at the same time. The judge briefly questioned the lawyers of both parties and then announced: "Today, the plaintiff did not appear. Wait for a rescheduled date. The plaintiff must appear in person to facilitate interrogation and verification."

Xu Zhaoquan's One Fall Became an Eternal Regret; Miao Fuquan is Suspected of Committing a Crime 213

Xu Zhaoquan, a 35-year-old man from Wuxi, was a waiter at the Hongyun Restaurant opened by Qian Zhengfu at No. 1103 Hanbil Road. At around 9:00 p.m. the night before, his colleague Miao Fuquan was cooking vegetables, and Xu嫌其手脚迟缓责, slightly rebuked him for being slow. Miao also refused to accept, so the two quarreled with each other. At that time, the owner of the restaurant returned from outside and learned the details of the dispute. He concluded that Miao was wrong, slapped him on the forehead, and ordered him to leave the restaurant immediately. Miao felt even more resentful after listening to the words, and went forward to argue with Xu. Suddenly, the two began to wrestle with each other. However, at that time, Xu was standing on a step ladder. For some reason, he could not stand firm and fell to the ground. Unexpectedly, after falling to the ground, he lost consciousness. Later, the owner of the restaurant sent him to Tongren Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. He died soon after. The hospital reported to the Hongkou Patrol Station, which ordered Detective Zhang Shoushan to investigate. Miao was arrested and detained at the patrol station. Xu's body was taken to the Ferrer Body Inspection Office. Yesterday morning, the report was sent to the First Special District Local Court. Prosecutor Guo Wei went to the office to examine the body and questioned the witnesses Wan Arong and Zhao Agou, who claimed that they saw the two arguing and wrestling with each other at that time. Xu suddenly fell to the ground from a step ladder and lost consciousness. Miao Fuquan, 21 years old, also claimed that there was an argument at that time, but he did not wrestle with him, and claimed that he did not know how he fell. The rest of the confessions were vague. Mr. Guo obtained the confession and then announced that the deceased Xu Zhaoquan was a male and died from a head injury sustained before his death. Miao Fuquan was suspected of committing a crime and should be prosecuted by the patrol station and sent to the court for review. The body was handed over to his wife, Xu Ma, who signed a guarantee to take it back for burial.

After Repeated Examinations, Yang Cuidi is Still a Virgin; Those Who Snatched the Bride are Sentenced Separately 214

Ni Haisheng, a farmer from Haimen, who lived at No. 653 Fahua Township, Jing'an Temple Road, and his eldest son Qingfu, and second son Jifu also followed their father in farming for a living, and their family was extremely impoverished. In the 10th year of the Republic of China, Jifu and Yang Wang's daughter Cuidi, who is now 22 years old, were engaged. Later, due to poverty, disputes arose, and they could not get married. The Yang woman and her daughter came to Shanghai and recently lived in a workshop in the Yufeng Yarn Factory on Dinghai Road. Cuidi worked in the factory and earned money to support herself, unwilling to be Ni's wife. At around 6:00 a.m. on the 28th of last month, Ni Haisheng and his three sons hired a car from the Xiangxing Company on Yuwei Road and parked it near the factory, in accordance with the rural custom of snatching the bride. When Ms. Yang finished her night shift and went out, she was dragged into the car by the Ni family, intending to drive her home to get married. The woman cried out for help. The driver, Huang Ayuan, saw that the situation was not good and drove the car to the General Patrol Station on Fuzhou Road. After questioning, he learned that it was a marital dispute. Due to the location of the incident, he ordered the thousand people to be transferred to the Yangshupu Patrol Station. Ni Haisheng and his sons, seeing that the matter had become stiff, lied that Ms. Yang was Jifu's wife, whom they had married on the 12th day of the first month of this year. After living together for about three months, the woman secretly fled to Shanghai. They asked her to go home, but Ms. Yang denied that she was married to Jifu and that there was no engagement or marriage. If they did not believe it, she was still a virgin. The patrol head, seeing that the circumstances were bizarre, sent the woman to the Sacred Heart Hospital. After the doctor's examination, it was confirmed that she was indeed a virgin. The Ni family was detained. Later, wedding red posts and letters were found at the Ni family's home, so they were sent to the First Special District Court. Under questioning, both parties insisted on their own versions. The defendant insisted that Jifu and Ms. Yang were actually married on the 12th day of the first month. The case was peculiar, and the court ordered it to be reviewed again at a later date. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zehan came to the Criminal Court No. 3 to continue the trial. Zhang Tianyin, a lawyer from the patrol station, stated that the red post for the engagement between Ms. Yang and Ni Jifu in this case was not forged. Perhaps the woman's mother regretted the engagement because she disliked the Ni family's poverty. The defendant's snatching of the bride was a common occurrence in rural customs, and they did not know that they had violated the criminal law. There was actually no marriage. The defendant insisted that Ms. Yang and Jifu were actually married on the 12th day of the first month, while Yang Wang and her daughter Cuidi completely denied it. For the sake of caution, the court ordered the woman to be re-examined by a medical doctor. The result was still that she was a virgin. Cuidi requested that the defendants be punished. Judge Wu then sentenced the three defendants, Ni Haisheng, etc., to three months of imprisonment each. Jifu and Qingfu were given a two-year suspended sentence.

The Young Women's Monthly Magazine Will Be Reformed Next Year

Zhou Longbao Died from Electric Shock

Recently, the Hefeng Yarn Factory in Wusong Yuncao Creek was adding walls. A plasterer, Zhou Longbao, 27 years old, a local, was building the wall yesterday when a wire broke and fell. Zhou's finger touched the wire, and his body fell, killing him instantly. The Seventh District First Precinct was notified, and they instructed the local guarantor, Zhou Lansheng, to report to the local court for examination.

An Unmarried Couple Seeking Fun Was Lightly Punished

Li Juan, a 21-year-old Ningbo woman residing at No. 35 Guangqi Road in the city, is fond of fashion and loves modernity. Yesterday morning, Li was holding a young man's arm, walking together on Fuyou Road. On the way, they hugged and kissed, performing their ballroom dance. This aroused applause and cheers from a group of idlers, disturbing public order. Cao Jinbao, of the Ninth Post of the Second Precinct of the First District, saw this and, considering that they should not have such obscene behavior that hinders public morals, immediately stepped forward to stop them. Unexpectedly, the man and woman refused to stop. They were immediately taken to the precinct for questioning. After questioning by the precinct chief, the defendant confessed his name as Chuan Fengtai, a 21-year-old Ningbo native who is a tea merchant, residing at No. 2 Zhengjia Muqiao in the French Concession. Li Juan is my fiancée, and we have a very good relationship, he said. Li Juan's confession was the same. The precinct chief, considering that the man and woman were engaging in obscene behavior on the road, related to public morals, and out of consideration for their ignorance, lightly punished them and let them go.

Zhou Tao Stole a Leather Coat While Using the Toilet

Zhou Tao, 23 years old, from Pudong, a woman who secretly engages in prostitution in various amusement parks such as the Small World and Great World, went to the women's restroom in Small World at 6:00 PM the other day. She told Xu Zhang, the woman in charge of the restroom, to get some face water to wash her hands and put on makeup. There was a fashionable leather coat hanging in the restroom, which belonged to Ms. Yuan, the head of the waitresses in the World, who had left it there for safekeeping. Unexpectedly, Zhou Tao took advantage of the fact that the restroom attendant was out getting water and stole the coat, wearing it away. When Xu Zhang returned with the water, she saw that the female guest had left. She looked around the room and saw that the coat Ms. Yuan had left for safekeeping had disappeared. She realized that it had been stolen by Zhou Tao. She immediately notified Ms. Yuan and searched for it everywhere, but found no trace. Later, she found the stolen coat at a pawnshop near Nanyang Bridge, having been pawned for seven dollars. Yesterday afternoon, at about 6:00 PM, Ms. Yuan ordered Xu Zhang to continue searching everywhere and found her at the Great Thousand World. Zhou Tao admitted to stealing the coat and pawning it for seven dollars, but said that she had lost the pawn ticket. Xu Zhang took Zhou Tao to the city and turned her over to the Second Precinct of the First District for investigation. After questioning by Precinct Chief Liu, she was sentenced to be sent to the General Bureau for legal action.
